<!-- Global Utility Functions -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
      // Make getPageName globally accessible for Adobe Launch Script and other scripts
      window.getPageName = function() {
          const urlSegments = location.pathname.split('/').filter(segment => segment.trim());
          return urlSegments.length >= 3 ? urlSegments[2] : 'home';
      };
  </script>

  <!-- STEP 1: Bot Selection Control -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
      (function() {
          'use strict';

          function getCookie(name) {
              const cookie = document.cookie.split('; ').find(c => c.startsWith(name + '='));
              return cookie ? decodeURIComponent(cookie.split('=')[1]) : '';
          }

          // CRITICAL: Make decision function reusable and globally accessible
          window.evaluateBotDecision = function evaluateBotDecision() {
              const portalSearchName = getCookie('apex__portalSearchName');
              const cspUserLocale = (getCookie('csp_user_locale') || 'en_US').replace(/-/g, '_').trim();

              // Check if current page should always use standard bot
              const pageName = window.getPageName();
              const overridePages = ['tech-master-support', 'business'];
              const shouldUseStandardBot = overridePages.includes(pageName);

              // Override: Show standard bot on specific pages even if cookie is agenticSearch
              const shouldShowAgentforce = (portalSearchName === 'agenticSearch' && cspUserLocale === 'en_US' && !shouldUseStandardBot);

              window.__SHOW_AGENTFORCE__ = shouldShowAgentforce;
              window.__SHOW_STANDARD_BOT__ = !shouldShowAgentforce;

              return shouldShowAgentforce;
          }

          // Evaluate initially
          const shouldShowAgentforce = window.evaluateBotDecision();

          if (shouldShowAgentforce) {
              // Don't block anything for Agentforce
              window.__STANDARD_BOT_DISABLED__ = true;

          } else {

              window.__AGENTFORCE_DISABLED__ = true;
              window.__STOP_REMOVING_ELEMENTS__ = false;

              // Hide Agentforce ONLY (not standard Einstein bot)
              const style = document.createElement('style');
              style.id = 'agentforce-blocker-style';
              style.innerHTML = `
                  embeddedmessaging-embedded-messaging[data-component-id*="SearchAgent"],
                  c-embedded-messaging[data-component-id*="SearchAgent"],
                  embeddedmessaging-embedded-messaging[data-component-id*="agentforceBot"],
                  c-embedded-messaging[data-component-id*="agentforceBot"] {
                      display: none !important;
                      visibility: hidden !important;
                  }
              `;
              document.head.appendChild(style);

              const removeAgentforceLightningComponentOnly = () => {
                  if (window.__STOP_REMOVING_ELEMENTS__) {
                      return false;
                  }

                  const selectors = [
                      'embeddedmessaging-embedded-messaging',
                      'c-embedded-messaging'
                  ];

                  let removed = 0;
                  selectors.forEach(selector => {
                      document.querySelectorAll(selector).forEach(el => {
                          const componentId = el.getAttribute('data-component-id') || '';
                          // ONLY remove Agentforce (SearchAgent), NOT standard bot (embeddedMessaging)
                          if (componentId.includes('SearchAgent')) {
                              console.log('🗑️ Removing Agentforce component:', componentId);
                              el.remove();
                              removed++;
                          }
                      });
                  });

                  return removed > 0;
              };

              removeAgentforceLightningComponentOnly();

              const removalInterval = setInterval(() => {
                  if (window.__STOP_REMOVING_ELEMENTS__) {
                      clearInterval(removalInterval);
                      return;
                  }
                  removeAgentforceLightningComponentOnly();
              }, 100);

              window.__ALLOW_STANDARD_BOT__ = function() {
                  window.__STOP_REMOVING_ELEMENTS__ = true;
              };

              let bootstrapBlocked = true;
              Object.defineProperty(window, 'embeddedservice_bootstrap', {
                  get: function() {
                      if (bootstrapBlocked) {
                          return {
                              settings: {},
                              init: function() {
                                  console.log('🚫 Blocked init()');
                              }
                          };
                      }
                      return window.__real_embeddedservice_bootstrap__;
                  },
                  set: function(value) {
                      if (!bootstrapBlocked) {
                          window.__real_embeddedservice_bootstrap__ = value;
                      } 
                  },
                  configurable: true
              });

              window.__UNBLOCK_BOOTSTRAP__ = function() {
                  window.__ALLOW_STANDARD_BOT__();
                  bootstrapBlocked = false;

                  try {
                      delete window.embeddedservice_bootstrap;
                      delete window.__real_embeddedservice_bootstrap__;
                  } catch (e) {
                      console.error('⚠️ Error unblocking:', e);
                  }
              };
          }

          // ============================================================
          // NEW: Listen for cookie changes and re-evaluate
          // ============================================================
          let lastCookieValue = getCookie('apex__portalSearchName');

          const checkCookieInterval = setInterval(() => {
              const currentCookieValue = getCookie('apex__portalSearchName');

              if (currentCookieValue && currentCookieValue !== lastCookieValue) {
                  lastCookieValue = currentCookieValue;

                  // Re-evaluate decision
                  const newDecision = window.evaluateBotDecision();

                  // If decision changed, reload page to apply correct bot
                  if (newDecision !== shouldShowAgentforce) {

                      // Check if we already reloaded
                      const reloadFlag = sessionStorage.getItem('apex__botReload');
                      if (reloadFlag !== 'true') {
                          sessionStorage.setItem('apex__botReload', 'true');
                          window.location.reload();
                      } else {
                          sessionStorage.removeItem('apex__botReload');
                      }
                  }
              }
          }, 200); // Check every 200ms for first 5 seconds

          // Stop checking after 5 seconds (cookie should be set by then)
          setTimeout(() => {
              clearInterval(checkCookieInterval);
          }, 5000);

      })();
  </script>

  <!-- Agentforce Retracting Fix Code START --->
  <script>
      // Track if onEmbeddedMessagingReady has been called before
      window.agentforce_ready_count = window.agentforce_ready_count || 0;

      window.addEventListener("onEmbeddedMessagingReady", () => {
          embeddedservice_bootstrap.settings.disableStreamingResponses = true;

          // Get cookie value
          function getCookie(name) {
              const cookie = document.cookie.split('; ').find(c => c.startsWith(name + '='));
              return cookie ? decodeURIComponent(cookie.split('=')[1]) : '';
          }

          // Check if this is Agentforce mode
          const portalSearchName = getCookie('apex__portalSearchName');
          const cspUserLocale = (getCookie('csp_user_locale') || 'en_US').replace(/-/g, '_').trim();
          const isAgentforceMode = portalSearchName === 'agenticSearch' && cspUserLocale === 'en_US';

          // Increment ready count
          window.agentforce_ready_count++;

          // If this is the second+ time onEmbeddedMessagingReady fires, it means conversation was ended
          if (isAgentforceMode && window.agentforce_ready_count > 1) {
              console.log('[Agentforce Ready] Detected conversation end via onEmbeddedMessagingReady (call #' + window.agentforce_ready_count + ')');
              // Dispatch a custom event to signal conversation ended
              window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('agentforce_conversation_reset'));
          }

          if (isAgentforceMode) {
              console.log('[Agentforce Ready] Checking for authenticated user email...');
              console.log('[Agentforce Ready] $A available:', typeof $A !== 'undefined');
              console.log('[Agentforce Ready] embeddedservice_bootstrap available:', typeof embeddedservice_bootstrap !== 'undefined');

              // Check if $A is available
              if (typeof $A === 'undefined') {
                  console.error('[Agentforce Ready] ❌ $A is not defined - cannot get user email');
                  return;
              }

              // Get authenticated user email (same as Einstein bot)
              const userEmail = $A.get('$SObjectType.CurrentUser.Email');
              const userId = $A.get('$SObjectType.CurrentUser.Id');

              console.log('[Agentforce Ready] User Email from $A:', userEmail);
              console.log('[Agentforce Ready] User ID from $A:', userId);

              if (userEmail && userEmail !== '' && userEmail !== 'null' && userId && userId !== '') {
                  console.log('[Agentforce Ready] ✅ Setting authenticated user email:', userEmail);

                  try {
                      embeddedservice_bootstrap.prechatAPI.setHiddenPrechatFields({
                          UserEmail: userEmail,
                          isAuthenticated: true,
                          siteUserId: userId
                      });
                      console.log('[Agentforce Ready] ✅ setHiddenPrechatFields called successfully');
                  } catch (error) {
                      console.error('[Agentforce Ready] ❌ Error setting email:', error);
                  }
              } else {
                  console.log('[Agentforce Ready] Anonymous user - userEmail:', userEmail, 'userId:', userId);
                  // Set as anonymous explicitly
                  try {
                      embeddedservice_bootstrap.prechatAPI.setHiddenPrechatFields({
                          UserEmail: '',
                          isAuthenticated: false,
                          siteUserId: ''
                      });
                      console.log('[Agentforce Ready] ✅ Set anonymous user fields');
                  } catch (error) {
                      console.error('[Agentforce Ready] ❌ Error setting anonymous fields:', error);
                  }
              }
          }
      });
  </script>
  <!-- Agentforce Retracting Fix Code END  --->
  
  <!-- Agentic AI knowledge search START - Simplified chat launch -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
      // Set page name as data attribute on body
      (function() {
          // Use global getPageName function
          const getPageName = window.getPageName;

          const setPageDataAttribute = () => {
              const pageName = getPageName();
              document.body.setAttribute('data-page-name', pageName);
          };

          // Set on load
          if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
              document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', setPageDataAttribute);
          } else {
              setPageDataAttribute();
          }

          // Update on URL changes (for SPA navigation)
          let previousUrl = location.href;
          const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
              if (location.href !== previousUrl) {
                  previousUrl = location.href;
                  setPageDataAttribute();
              }
          });

          observer.observe(document, { subtree: true, childList: true });
      })();
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
      // ============================================================
      // MODAL OVERLAY: Allow Tab in chat, block Tab on background
      // ONLY FOR AGENTICSEARCH VARIATION
      // ============================================================
      (function() {
          'use strict';

          var chatOverlay = null;
          var lastFocusedElement = null;
          var overlayActive = false;
          var focusMonitorInterval = null;

          /**
           * Get cookie value
           */
          function getCookie(name) {
              var cookies = document.cookie.split('; ');
              for (var i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {
                  var parts = cookies[i].split('=');
                  if (parts[0] === name) {
                      return decodeURIComponent(parts[1]);
                  }
              }
              return null;
          }

          // Use global getPageName function
          const getPageName = window.getPageName;

          // Check if current page should always use standard bot
          const shouldUseStandardBotForPage = () => {
              const pageName = getPageName();
              const overridePages = ['tech-master-support', 'business']; // Pages that always use standard bot
              const isOverridePage = overridePages.includes(pageName);
              return isOverridePage;
          };

          /**
           * Check if current variation is agenticSearch
           */
          function isAgenticSearch() {
              // Check global flag first
              if (typeof window.__SHOW_AGENTFORCE__ !== 'undefined') {
                  return window.__SHOW_AGENTFORCE__;
              }

              // Fallback to cookie check
              var portalVariation = getCookie('apex__portalSearchName');
              var portalLanguage = getCookie('apex__portalLanguage');

              // Override: Show standard bot on specific pages
              if (shouldUseStandardBotForPage()) {
                  return false; // Don't use agentic modal
              }

              if(portalVariation == 'agenticSearch' && portalLanguage.startsWith('en')){
                  return portalVariation === 'agenticSearch';
              }

              return false;
          }

          /**
           * Get chat elements
           */
          function getChatElements() {
              var frame = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingFrame');
              var iframe = frame ? frame.querySelector('iframe') : null;
              var button = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingConversationButton');

              return {
                  frame: frame,
                  iframe: iframe,
                  button: button
              };
          }

          /**
           * Check if element is chat
           */
          function isElementChat(element) {
              if (!element) return false;

              var chat = getChatElements();

              return element === chat.iframe ||
                     element === chat.frame ||
                     element === chat.button ||
                     (chat.frame && chat.frame.contains(element)) ||
                     element.id === 'chat-modal-overlay';
          }

          /**
           * Smart Tab blocker: Allow Tab in iframe, block on background
           */
          function smartTabBlocker(event) {
              if (!overlayActive) return;

              // Only handle Tab key
              if (event.key !== 'Tab' && event.keyCode !== 9) return;

              var activeElement = document.activeElement;
              var chat = getChatElements();

              // If focus is on iframe, ALLOW Tab (iframe handles it internally)
              if (activeElement === chat.iframe || activeElement === chat.frame) {
                  return; // Do nothing, let iframe handle Tab
              }

              // If focus is on chat button, ALLOW Tab to move to iframe
              if (activeElement === chat.button) {
                  event.preventDefault();
                  if (chat.iframe) {
                      chat.iframe.focus();
                  }
                  return;
              }

              // If focus is anywhere else (background), BLOCK Tab
              event.preventDefault();
              event.stopPropagation();
              event.stopImmediatePropagation();

              // Force focus to iframe
              if (chat.iframe) {
                  chat.iframe.focus();
              } else if (chat.button) {
                  chat.button.focus();
              }

              return false;
          }

          /**
           * Block other keyboard events on background
           */
          function blockBackgroundKeys(event) {
              if (!overlayActive) return;

              var activeElement = document.activeElement;
              var chat = getChatElements();

              // Allow all keyboard in chat
              if (activeElement === chat.iframe ||
                  activeElement === chat.frame ||
                  activeElement === chat.button) {
                  return;
              }

              // Block on background
              if (activeElement !== document.body && activeElement !== document.documentElement) {
                  event.preventDefault();
                  event.stopPropagation();
                  event.stopImmediatePropagation();
                  return false;
              }
          }

          /**
           * Monitor focus escaping and force it back
           */
          function startFocusMonitoring() {
              if (focusMonitorInterval) return;

              focusMonitorInterval = setInterval(function() {
                  if (!overlayActive) return;

                  var activeElement = document.activeElement;
                  var chat = getChatElements();

                  // Allow focus on iframe, button, body
                  var focusOK = activeElement === chat.iframe ||
                               activeElement === chat.frame ||
                               activeElement === chat.button ||
                               activeElement === document.body ||
                               activeElement === document.documentElement;

                  if (!focusOK) {

                      // Force back to iframe
                      if (chat.iframe) {
                          chat.iframe.focus();
                      }
                  }
              }, 50); // Check every 50ms

          }

          /**
           * Stop focus monitoring
           */
          function stopFocusMonitoring() {
              if (focusMonitorInterval) {
                  clearInterval(focusMonitorInterval);
                  focusMonitorInterval = null;
              }
          }

          /**
           * Disable background elements
           */
          function disableBackground() {
              var chat = getChatElements();
              var overlay = document.getElementById('chat-modal-overlay');

              var allElements = document.querySelectorAll('a, button, input, textarea, select, [tabindex], [contenteditable="true"]');
              var count = 0;

              allElements.forEach(function(el) {
                  // Skip chat elements
                  if (isElementChat(el) || el === overlay) {
                      return;
                  }

                  // Store and disable
                  var currentTabIndex = el.getAttribute('tabindex');
                  el.setAttribute('data-original-tabindex', currentTabIndex || 'none');
                  el.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1');
                  el.setAttribute('inert', '');
                  el.style.pointerEvents = 'none';

                  count++;
              });

          }

          /**
           * Restore background elements
           */
          function restoreBackground() {
              var elements = document.querySelectorAll('[data-original-tabindex]');

              elements.forEach(function(el) {
                  var original = el.getAttribute('data-original-tabindex');

                  if (original === 'none') {
                      el.removeAttribute('tabindex');
                  } else {
                      el.setAttribute('tabindex', original);
                  }

                  el.removeAttribute('data-original-tabindex');
                  el.removeAttribute('inert');
                  el.style.pointerEvents = '';
              });

          }

          /**
           * Show overlay
           */
          function showChatOverlay() {
              if (chatOverlay) return;

              overlayActive = true;

              // Disable background
              disableBackground();

              // Start focus monitoring
              startFocusMonitoring();

              // Create overlay
              chatOverlay = document.createElement('div');
              chatOverlay.id = 'chat-modal-overlay';
              chatOverlay.style.cssText = `
                  position: fixed;
                  top: 0;
                  left: 0;
                  width: 100%;
                  height: 100%;
                  background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.5);
                  z-index: 9998;
                  display: block;
                  backdrop-filter: blur(2px);
                  cursor: not-allowed;
                  pointer-events: auto;
              `;

              chatOverlay.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                  e.preventDefault();
                  e.stopPropagation();
              });

              document.body.appendChild(chatOverlay);
              document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';

              // Make chat visible above overlay
              var chat = getChatElements();

              if (chat.frame) {
                  chat.frame.style.zIndex = '9999';
                  chat.frame.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
              }
              if (chat.button) {
                  chat.button.style.zIndex = '9999';
                  chat.button.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
              }
              if (chat.iframe) {
                  chat.iframe.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';

                  // Focus iframe
                  setTimeout(function() {
                      chat.iframe.focus();
                  }, 100);
              }

          }

          /**
           * Hide overlay
           */
          function hideChatOverlay() {
              if (!chatOverlay) return;

              overlayActive = false;

              stopFocusMonitoring();
              restoreBackground();

              if (chatOverlay.parentNode) {
                  chatOverlay.parentNode.removeChild(chatOverlay);
              }
              chatOverlay = null;

              document.body.style.overflow = '';

              if (lastFocusedElement && typeof lastFocusedElement.focus === 'function') {
                  try {
                      lastFocusedElement.focus();
                  } catch (e) {}
              }
              lastFocusedElement = null;
          }

          /**
           * Check if chat is open
           */
          function isChatOpen() {
              var chatFrame = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingFrame');
              if (chatFrame) {
                  // Check Salesforce's isMinimized class
                  var isMinimized = chatFrame.classList.contains('isMinimized');
                  return !isMinimized;
              }
              return false;
          }

          /**
           * Allow chat to open (remove our restrictions)
           */
          function allowChatToOpen() {
              console.log('💬 [Allow] User clicked chat button - allowing it to open');

              // Clear the minimize flag
              window.agentforce_should_minimize = false;

              // Set flag to prevent focus handler from re-minimizing
              window.agentforce_just_allowed_open = true;

              // Clear the flag after 2 seconds (enough time for chat to open)
              setTimeout(function() {
                  window.agentforce_just_allowed_open = false;
                  console.log('💬 [Allow] Cleared "just allowed" flag');
              }, 2000);

              // Stop the watcher
              if (minimizeWatchInterval) {
                  clearInterval(minimizeWatchInterval);
                  minimizeWatchInterval = null;
              }

              // Remove our data attribute
              var chatFrame = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingFrame');
              if (chatFrame) {
                  chatFrame.removeAttribute('data-agentforce-minimize');
                  console.log('💬 [Allow] Removed minimize attribute, chat can now open');
              }

              // Update localStorage - this tab now owns the chat
              try {
                  localStorage.setItem('agentforce_chat_state', JSON.stringify({
                      tabId: window.agentforce_tab_id,
                      timestamp: Date.now(),
                      open: true
                  }));
                  console.log('💬 [Allow] Updated localStorage - this tab owns the chat');
              } catch (e) {
                  console.error('Error updating chat state:', e);
              }
          }

          /**
           * Minimize chat by clicking the main chat button (toggles chat)
           */
          function minimizeChat() {
              try {
                  console.log('💬 [minimizeChat] Attempting to minimize chat...');
                  var chat = getChatElements();

                  if (!chat.frame) {
                      console.log('💬 [minimizeChat] ⚠️ Chat frame not found yet');
                      return false;
                  }

                  if (!chat.button) {
                      console.log('💬 [minimizeChat] ⚠️ Chat button not found');
                      return false;
                  }

                  // Check if chat is actually open
                  var isOpen = !chat.frame.classList.contains('isMinimized');

                  if (!isOpen) {
                      console.log('💬 [minimizeChat] Chat is already minimized');
                      window.agentforce_last_minimize_time = Date.now();
                      return true;
                  }

                  console.log('💬 [minimizeChat] Clicking chat button to minimize');

                  // Click the main chat button - this should toggle/minimize the chat
                  chat.button.click();

                  // Track when we minimized
                  window.agentforce_last_minimize_time = Date.now();

                  // Verify it minimized after a short delay
                  setTimeout(function() {
                      var frame = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingFrame');
                      if (frame && frame.classList.contains('isMinimized')) {
                          console.log('💬 [minimizeChat] ✅ Successfully minimized!');
                          // Start watcher to prevent re-opening
                          startMinimizeWatch(frame);
                      } else {
                          console.log('💬 [minimizeChat] ⚠️ Still open after clicking, retrying...');
                          // Try clicking again
                          var chatElements = getChatElements();
                          if (chatElements.button) {
                              chatElements.button.click();
                              window.agentforce_last_minimize_time = Date.now();

                              // Final verification
                              setTimeout(function() {
                                  var finalFrame = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingFrame');
                                  if (finalFrame && finalFrame.classList.contains('isMinimized')) {
                                      console.log('💬 [minimizeChat] ✅ Minimized on second try!');
                                      startMinimizeWatch(finalFrame);
                                  } else {
                                      console.log('💬 [minimizeChat] ⚠️ Could not minimize, using fallback');
                                      // Fallback: force with CSS
                                      if (finalFrame) {
                                          finalFrame.setAttribute('data-agentforce-minimize', 'true');
                                          finalFrame.classList.add('isMinimized');
                                      }
                                      startMinimizeWatch(finalFrame);
                                  }
                              }, 500);
                          }
                      }
                  }, 500);

                  return true;
              } catch (e) {
                  console.error('💬 [minimizeChat] ❌ Error:', e);
                  return false;
              }
          }

          /**
           * Generate unique tab ID
           */
          if (!window.agentforce_tab_id) {
              window.agentforce_tab_id = 'tab_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9);
              console.log('🆔 Tab ID:', window.agentforce_tab_id);
          }

          /**
           * Immediately hide chat if another tab has it open
           */
          (function immediateHide() {
              try {
                  var chatState = localStorage.getItem('agentforce_chat_state');
                  if (chatState) {
                      var state = JSON.parse(chatState);
                      var isRecent = (Date.now() - state.timestamp) < 30000;

                      if (state.open && state.tabId !== window.agentforce_tab_id && isRecent) {
                          console.log('💬 [Immediate Hide] Chat open in another tab, adding CSS to hide chat');
                          window.agentforce_should_minimize = true;

                          // Add temporary CSS to hide chat until we can click the minimize button
                          var style = document.createElement('style');
                          style.id = 'agentforce-temp-hide';
                          style.innerHTML = `
                              /* Temporarily hide chat window while not minimized (fallback only) */
                              .embeddedMessagingFrame:not(.isMinimized)[data-agentforce-minimize="true"] {
                                  /* Hide the chat content */
                                  opacity: 0 !important;
                                  visibility: hidden !important;
                                  pointer-events: none !important;
                              }

                              /* Hide iframe inside */
                              .embeddedMessagingFrame[data-agentforce-minimize="true"] iframe {
                                  display: none !important;
                              }

                              /* CRITICAL: Keep button visible and clickable */
                              .embeddedMessagingConversationButton {
                                  display: block !important;
                                  pointer-events: auto !important;
                                  visibility: visible !important;
                                  opacity: 1 !important;
                                  z-index: 9999 !important;
                              }
                          `;

                          // Insert at the very beginning of head to ensure it takes precedence
                          if (document.head.firstChild) {
                              document.head.insertBefore(style, document.head.firstChild);
                          } else {
                              document.head.appendChild(style);
                          }

                          console.log('💬 [Immediate Hide] Permanent minimize CSS applied');
                      }
                  }
              } catch (e) {
                  console.error('Error in immediate hide:', e);
              }
          })();

          /**
           * Keep watching to detect if chat tries to open automatically
           */
          var minimizeWatchInterval = null;

          function startMinimizeWatch(chatFrame) {
              if (minimizeWatchInterval) {
                  return; // Already watching
              }

              console.log('💬 [Watch] Starting minimize watcher');

              minimizeWatchInterval = setInterval(function() {
                  if (!window.agentforce_should_minimize) {
                      // Stop watching if we don't need to minimize anymore
                      clearInterval(minimizeWatchInterval);
                      minimizeWatchInterval = null;
                      console.log('💬 [Watch] Stopped minimize watcher - minimize mode off');
                      return;
                  }

                  var frame = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingFrame');
                  if (frame && !frame.classList.contains('isMinimized')) {
                      // Check if this is user action or automatic
                      var timeSinceMinimize = Date.now() - (window.agentforce_last_minimize_time || 0);

                      if (timeSinceMinimize > 2000) {
                          // More than 2 seconds since last minimize = user opened it
                          console.log('💬 [Watch] User opened chat, stopping watcher');
                          window.agentforce_should_minimize = false;
                          clearInterval(minimizeWatchInterval);
                          minimizeWatchInterval = null;
                          return;
                      }

                      // Less than 2 seconds = automatic opening, click minimize button again
                      console.log('💬 [Watch] Chat trying to auto-open! Re-minimizing...');
                      minimizeChat();
                      window.agentforce_last_minimize_time = Date.now();
                  }
              }, 500); // Check every 500ms
          }

          /**
           * Update localStorage with current chat state
           */
          function updateChatState(isOpen) {
              try {
                  if (isOpen) {
                      // Check if another tab already has chat open
                      var existingState = localStorage.getItem('agentforce_chat_state');
                      if (existingState) {
                          var state = JSON.parse(existingState);
                          var isRecent = (Date.now() - state.timestamp) < 30000;

                          // If another tab has chat open recently, don't update - let this tab minimize
                          if (state.open && state.tabId !== window.agentforce_tab_id && isRecent) {
                              console.log('💬 Chat already open in Tab:', state.tabId, '- not updating state');
                              return;
                          }
                      }

                      // Update state with this tab's info
                      localStorage.setItem('agentforce_chat_state', JSON.stringify({
                          tabId: window.agentforce_tab_id,
                          timestamp: Date.now(),
                          open: true
                      }));
                  } else {
                      // Only clear if this tab was the one that opened it
                      var currentState = localStorage.getItem('agentforce_chat_state');
                      if (currentState) {
                          var state = JSON.parse(currentState);
                          if (state.tabId === window.agentforce_tab_id) {
                              localStorage.setItem('agentforce_chat_state', JSON.stringify({
                                  tabId: window.agentforce_tab_id,
                                  timestamp: Date.now(),
                                  open: false
                              }));
                          }
                      }
                  }
              } catch (e) {
                  console.error('Error updating chat state:', e);
              }
          }

          /**
           * Persistent monitoring interval reference
           */
          var persistentMonitorInterval = null;

          /**
           * Start persistent monitoring for chat opening - with retries to click minimize button
           */
          function startPersistentMonitoring() {
              if (persistentMonitorInterval) {
                  clearInterval(persistentMonitorInterval);
              }

              console.log('💬 Starting persistent monitoring for chat window');
              var checkCount = 0;
              var maxChecks = 60; // Monitor for 30 seconds (60 * 500ms)
              var minimizeAttempts = 0;
              var maxMinimizeAttempts = 10;

              persistentMonitorInterval = setInterval(function() {
                  checkCount++;

                  // Stop after max checks
                  if (checkCount > maxChecks) {
                      clearInterval(persistentMonitorInterval);
                      persistentMonitorInterval = null;
                      console.log('💬 Stopped persistent monitoring after', maxChecks * 0.5, 'seconds');
                      return;
                  }

                  // Check localStorage state
                  try {
                      var chatState = localStorage.getItem('agentforce_chat_state');
                      if (chatState) {
                          var state = JSON.parse(chatState);
                          var isRecent = (Date.now() - state.timestamp) < 30000;

                          // If another tab has chat open
                          if (state.open && state.tabId !== window.agentforce_tab_id && isRecent) {
                              window.agentforce_should_minimize = true;

                              // Check if chat frame exists and is open
                              var chatFrame = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingFrame');
                              if (chatFrame && !chatFrame.classList.contains('isMinimized')) {
                                  minimizeAttempts++;

                                  if (minimizeAttempts <= maxMinimizeAttempts) {
                                      console.log('💬 [Persistent Monitor] Chat frame found, attempting to minimize (attempt', minimizeAttempts, ')');
                                      minimizeChat();

                                      // If successfully minimized, stop monitoring
                                      setTimeout(function() {
                                          if (!isChatOpen()) {
                                              clearInterval(persistentMonitorInterval);
                                              persistentMonitorInterval = null;
                                              console.log('💬 [Persistent Monitor] Successfully minimized, stopping');
                                          }
                                      }, 500);
                                  }
                              }
                          } else {
                              // No other tab has chat open, stop monitoring
                              window.agentforce_should_minimize = false;
                              clearInterval(persistentMonitorInterval);
                              persistentMonitorInterval = null;
                          }
                      }
                  } catch (e) {
                      console.error('Error in persistent monitor:', e);
                  }
              }, 500);
          }

          /**
           * Check if chat is already open in another tab on load
           */
          function checkExistingChatState() {
              try {
                  var chatState = localStorage.getItem('agentforce_chat_state');
                  if (chatState) {
                      var state = JSON.parse(chatState);
                      var isRecent = (Date.now() - state.timestamp) < 30000; // Within 30 seconds

                      if (state.open && state.tabId !== window.agentforce_tab_id && isRecent) {
                          console.log('💬 Chat is open in Tab:', state.tabId, '- THIS tab will minimize chat when it opens');
                          // Set a flag to minimize if chat opens
                          window.agentforce_should_minimize = true;

                          // Check immediately if chat frame exists
                          var chatFrame = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingFrame');
                          if (chatFrame) {
                              console.log('💬 Chat frame exists, attempting to minimize');

                              // Multiple attempts at different intervals
                              setTimeout(function() {
                                  if (window.agentforce_should_minimize) {
                                      console.log('💬 [checkExisting] Attempt 1');
                                      minimizeChat();
                                  }
                              }, 500);

                              setTimeout(function() {
                                  if (window.agentforce_should_minimize && isChatOpen()) {
                                      console.log('💬 [checkExisting] Attempt 2');
                                      minimizeChat();
                                  }
                              }, 1500);

                              setTimeout(function() {
                                  if (window.agentforce_should_minimize && isChatOpen()) {
                                      console.log('💬 [checkExisting] Attempt 3');
                                      minimizeChat();
                                  }
                              }, 3000);

                              return;
                          }

                          // Start persistent monitoring
                          startPersistentMonitoring();
                      }
                  }
              } catch (e) {
                  console.error('Error checking existing chat state:', e);
              }
          }

          /**
           * Monitor chat state
           */
          function monitorChatState() {
              // If we're forcefully minimizing, check if chat is opening
              if (window.agentforce_should_minimize) {
                  var chatFrame = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingFrame');

                  // If frame exists and is not minimized
                  if (chatFrame && !chatFrame.classList.contains('isMinimized')) {
                      // Check if it was opened by user (has been more than 2 seconds since we minimized)
                      var timeSinceMinimize = Date.now() - (window.agentforce_last_minimize_time || 0);

                      if (timeSinceMinimize > 2000) {
                          console.log('💬 [Monitor] Chat opened by user, allowing it');
                          // User opened it, so clear the minimize flag
                          window.agentforce_should_minimize = false;

                          // Stop the watcher
                          if (minimizeWatchInterval) {
                              clearInterval(minimizeWatchInterval);
                              minimizeWatchInterval = null;
                          }
                      }
                  }
                  return; // Don't run normal monitoring
              }

              var chatOpen = isChatOpen();

              if (chatOpen) {
                  showChatOverlay();
                  updateChatState(true);
              } else {
                  hideChatOverlay();
                  updateChatState(false);
              }
          }

          /**
           * Check on page visibility change (when user switches tabs)
           */
          document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', function() {
              if (!document.hidden && isAgenticSearch()) {
                  console.log('💬 [Visibility] Tab became visible, checking chat state');

                  // Don't minimize if user just opened chat
                  if (window.agentforce_just_allowed_open) {
                      console.log('💬 [Visibility] User just opened chat, skipping check');
                      return;
                  }

                  // Tab became visible, check if chat should be minimized
                  setTimeout(function() {
                      // Double check
                      if (window.agentforce_just_allowed_open) {
                          return;
                      }

                      var chatState = localStorage.getItem('agentforce_chat_state');
                      if (chatState) {
                          try {
                              var state = JSON.parse(chatState);
                              var isRecent = (Date.now() - state.timestamp) < 30000;

                              if (state.open && state.tabId !== window.agentforce_tab_id && isRecent) {
                                  console.log('💬 [Visibility] Chat open in Tab:', state.tabId);
                                  window.agentforce_should_minimize = true;

                                  var chatFrame = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingFrame');
                                  if (chatFrame) {
                                      console.log('💬 [Visibility] Chat frame exists, minimizing now!');
                                      minimizeChat();
                                  } else {
                                      console.log('💬 [Visibility] Chat not loaded yet, will minimize when it appears');
                                      startPersistentMonitoring();
                                  }
                              }
                          } catch (e) {
                              console.error('Error checking on visibility change:', e);
                          }
                      }
                  }, 100);
              }
          });

          /**
           * Check on window focus (when user clicks on the window)
           * But DON'T interfere if user just clicked to open chat
           */
          window.addEventListener('focus', function() {
              if (isAgenticSearch()) {
                  console.log('💬 [Focus] Window focused, checking chat state');

                  // Don't re-minimize if we just allowed chat to open
                  if (window.agentforce_just_allowed_open) {
                      console.log('💬 [Focus] User just opened chat, skipping minimize check');
                      return;
                  }

                  setTimeout(function() {
                      // Double check we didn't just allow opening
                      if (window.agentforce_just_allowed_open) {
                          console.log('💬 [Focus] User opened chat, skipping minimize');
                          return;
                      }

                      var chatState = localStorage.getItem('agentforce_chat_state');
                      if (chatState) {
                          try {
                              var state = JSON.parse(chatState);
                              var isRecent = (Date.now() - state.timestamp) < 30000;

                              if (state.open && state.tabId !== window.agentforce_tab_id && isRecent) {
                                  console.log('💬 [Focus] Chat open elsewhere, ensuring this one is minimized');
                                  window.agentforce_should_minimize = true;
                                  var chatFrame = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingFrame');
                                  if (chatFrame) {
                                      minimizeChat();
                                  }
                              }
                          } catch (e) {
                              console.error('Error on focus:', e);
                          }
                      }
                  }, 100);
              }
          });

          /**
           * Cleanup on page unload
           */
          window.addEventListener('beforeunload', function() {
              try {
                  // Stop the minimize watcher
                  if (minimizeWatchInterval) {
                      clearInterval(minimizeWatchInterval);
                      minimizeWatchInterval = null;
                  }

                  // Clear localStorage if this tab owns the chat
                  var chatState = localStorage.getItem('agentforce_chat_state');
                  if (chatState) {
                      var state = JSON.parse(chatState);
                      // Only clear if this tab was the owner
                      if (state.tabId === window.agentforce_tab_id && state.open) {
                          localStorage.removeItem('agentforce_chat_state');
                      }
                  }
              } catch (e) {
                  console.error('Error during cleanup:', e);
              }
          });

          /**
           * Intercept chat launch to keep it minimized
           */
          function interceptChatLaunch() {
              // Wait for embeddedservice_bootstrap to be available
              var checkInterval = setInterval(function() {
                  if (window.embeddedservice_bootstrap && window.embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI) {
                      clearInterval(checkInterval);

                      var originalLaunchChat = window.embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI.launchChat;

                      window.embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI.launchChat = function() {
                          console.log('💬 [Intercept] launchChat called');

                          // Check if we should minimize
                          var chatState = localStorage.getItem('agentforce_chat_state');
                          if (chatState) {
                              try {
                                  var state = JSON.parse(chatState);
                                  var isRecent = (Date.now() - state.timestamp) < 30000;

                                  if (state.open && state.tabId !== window.agentforce_tab_id && isRecent) {
                                      console.log('💬 [Intercept] Chat open in another tab - will minimize immediately after launch');
                                      window.agentforce_should_minimize = true;

                                      // Call original but immediately minimize
                                      var result = originalLaunchChat.apply(this, arguments);

                                      // Minimize as soon as chat opens
                                      setTimeout(function() {
                                          console.log('💬 [Intercept] Minimizing after launch');
                                          minimizeChat();
                                      }, 100);

                                      return result;
                                  }
                              } catch (e) {
                                  console.error('Error in launch intercept:', e);
                              }
                          }

                          // Normal launch
                          return originalLaunchChat.apply(this, arguments);
                      };

                      console.log('💬 [Intercept] Chat launch intercepted');
                  }
              }, 100);
          }

          /**
           * Initialize
           */
          function initialize() {
              if (!isAgenticSearch()) {
                  return;
              }

              // Intercept chat launch
              interceptChatLaunch();

              // Add smart blockers at window level with capture
              window.addEventListener('keydown', smartTabBlocker, true);
              window.addEventListener('keyup', blockBackgroundKeys, true);
              window.addEventListener('keypress', blockBackgroundKeys, true);

              console.log('✅ Smart blockers installed');
              console.log('✅ Cross-tab chat sync enabled for Tab ID:', window.agentforce_tab_id);

              // Check if chat is already open in another tab - do this early
              checkExistingChatState();

              // Setup chat button click listener to allow user to open chat
              (function setupChatButtonListener() {
                  var checkCount = 0;
                  var maxChecks = 40; // 20 seconds

                  var interval = setInterval(function() {
                      checkCount++;

                      var chatButton = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingConversationButton');
                      if (chatButton) {
                          clearInterval(interval);

                          console.log('💬 [Button Listener] Found chat button, adding click listener');

                          // Listen for clicks on the button
                          chatButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                              console.log('💬 [Button Click] User clicked chat button!');

                              // Check if we're in minimize mode
                              if (window.agentforce_should_minimize) {
                                  console.log('💬 [Button Click] Allowing chat to open in this tab');
                                  allowChatToOpen();
                              }
                          }, true); // Use capture phase to catch it early

                      } else if (checkCount > maxChecks) {
                          clearInterval(interval);
                          console.log('💬 [Button Listener] Stopped looking for chat button after 20 seconds');
                      }
                  }, 500);
              })();

              // Monitor chat state frequently
              setInterval(monitorChatState, 500);

              // Watch for chat frame being added to DOM
              var domObserver = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
                  if (!window.agentforce_should_minimize) {
                      return; // Exit early if we don't need to minimize
                  }

                  // Check for any chat-related elements
                  for (var i = 0; i < mutations.length; i++) {
                      var mutation = mutations[i];
                      if (mutation.addedNodes && mutation.addedNodes.length > 0) {
                          for (var j = 0; j < mutation.addedNodes.length; j++) {
                              var node = mutation.addedNodes[j];
                              if (node.nodeType === 1) { // Element node
                                  // Check if it's the chat frame or button
                                  if (node.classList && (
                                      node.classList.contains('embeddedMessagingFrame') ||
                                      node.classList.contains('embeddedMessagingConversationButton')
                                  )) {
                                      console.log('💬 [DOM Observer] Chat element added:', node.className);

                                      // Try to minimize multiple times
                                      setTimeout(function() {
                                          console.log('💬 [DOM Observer] Attempt 1 to minimize');
                                          minimizeChat();
                                      }, 500);

                                      setTimeout(function() {
                                          if (window.agentforce_should_minimize && isChatOpen()) {
                                              console.log('💬 [DOM Observer] Attempt 2 to minimize');
                                              minimizeChat();
                                          }
                                      }, 1500);

                                      setTimeout(function() {
                                          if (window.agentforce_should_minimize && isChatOpen()) {
                                              console.log('💬 [DOM Observer] Attempt 3 to minimize');
                                              minimizeChat();
                                          }
                                      }, 3000);

                                      return; // Stop after first match
                                  }

                                  // Check descendants
                                  if (node.querySelector) {
                                      var chatFrame = node.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingFrame');
                                      var chatButton = node.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingConversationButton');

                                      if (chatFrame || chatButton) {
                                          console.log('💬 [DOM Observer] Chat elements found in added node!');

                                          // Try to minimize with multiple attempts
                                          setTimeout(function() {
                                              minimizeChat();
                                          }, 500);

                                          setTimeout(function() {
                                              if (window.agentforce_should_minimize && isChatOpen()) {
                                                  minimizeChat();
                                              }
                                          }, 1500);

                                          return;
                                      }
                                  }
                              }
                          }
                      }
                  }
              });

              // Observe the entire document for chat elements being added
              domObserver.observe(document.body, {
                  childList: true,
                  subtree: true,
                  attributes: false
              });

              window.addEventListener('onEmbeddedMessagingReady', function() {
                  console.log('💬 [Event] Chat ready - checking if should minimize');

                  if (window.agentforce_should_minimize) {
                      // Multiple attempts to minimize
                      setTimeout(function() {
                          console.log('💬 [Event] Attempt 1 to minimize');
                          minimizeChat();
                      }, 500);

                      setTimeout(function() {
                          if (window.agentforce_should_minimize && isChatOpen()) {
                              console.log('💬 [Event] Attempt 2 to minimize');
                              minimizeChat();
                          }
                      }, 1500);

                      setTimeout(function() {
                          if (window.agentforce_should_minimize && isChatOpen()) {
                              console.log('💬 [Event] Attempt 3 to minimize');
                              minimizeChat();
                          }
                      }, 3000);
                  }
              });

              window.addEventListener('onEmbeddedMessagingConversationStarted', function() {
                  console.log('💬 [Event] Conversation started - checking if should minimize');

                  // Re-check state
                  var chatState = localStorage.getItem('agentforce_chat_state');
                  if (chatState) {
                      try {
                          var state = JSON.parse(chatState);
                          var isRecent = (Date.now() - state.timestamp) < 30000;

                          if (state.open && state.tabId !== window.agentforce_tab_id && isRecent) {
                              window.agentforce_should_minimize = true;
                          }
                      } catch (e) {
                          // Ignore
                      }
                  }

                  if (window.agentforce_should_minimize) {
                      // Minimize immediately when conversation starts
                      console.log('💬 [Event] Minimizing chat immediately after conversation started');
                      setTimeout(function() {
                          minimizeChat();
                      }, 50);
                  } else {
                      setTimeout(monitorChatState, 500);
                  }
              });

              var attributeObserver = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
                  mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
                      if (!window.agentforce_should_minimize) {
                          monitorChatState();
                          return;
                      }

                      var chatFrame = mutation.target;

                      // Watch for class changes - if chat opens when it shouldn't
                      if (mutation.attributeName === 'class') {
                          if (!chatFrame.classList.contains('isMinimized')) {
                              var timeSinceMinimize = Date.now() - (window.agentforce_last_minimize_time || 0);

                              if (timeSinceMinimize > 2000) {
                                  // User opened it
                                  console.log('💬 [Attribute Observer] User opened chat, stopping minimize mode');
                                  window.agentforce_should_minimize = false;
                                  return;
                              } else {
                                  // Auto-opened, click minimize button
                                  console.log('💬 [Attribute Observer] Chat auto-opened, re-minimizing');
                                  setTimeout(function() {
                                      minimizeChat();
                                  }, 200);
                              }
                          }
                      }
                  });
              });

              function observeChat() {
                  var chatFrame = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingFrame');
                  if (chatFrame) {
                      attributeObserver.observe(chatFrame, {
                          attributes: true,
                          attributeFilter: ['class', 'style', 'data-agentforce-minimize'],
                          attributeOldValue: true
                      });

                      // Check immediately when frame is found
                      if (window.agentforce_should_minimize) {
                          console.log('💬 [Observer Setup] Chat frame found, waiting to minimize');

                          // Wait for iframe to load
                          setTimeout(function() {
                              if (window.agentforce_should_minimize) {
                                  console.log('💬 [Observer Setup] Attempting to minimize chat');
                                  minimizeChat();
                              }
                          }, 1000);
                      }
                  } else {
                      setTimeout(observeChat, 500);
                  }
              }

              observeChat();
          }

          // Start checking immediately on script load
          (function earlyCheck() {
              if (!isAgenticSearch()) {
                  return;
              }

              console.log('💬 [Early Check] Script loaded, checking for existing chat state...');

              // Do an immediate check
              checkExistingChatState();

              // Multiple attempts to minimize chat at different times
              setTimeout(function() {
                  if (window.agentforce_should_minimize && isChatOpen()) {
                      console.log('💬 [Timed Check] Attempt at 500ms');
                      minimizeChat();
                  }
              }, 500);

              setTimeout(function() {
                  if (window.agentforce_should_minimize && isChatOpen()) {
                      console.log('💬 [Timed Check] Attempt at 1s');
                      minimizeChat();
                  }
              }, 1000);

              setTimeout(function() {
                  if (window.agentforce_should_minimize && isChatOpen()) {
                      console.log('💬 [Timed Check] Attempt at 2s');
                      minimizeChat();
                  }
              }, 2000);

              setTimeout(function() {
                  if (window.agentforce_should_minimize && isChatOpen()) {
                      console.log('💬 [Timed Check] Attempt at 3s');
                      minimizeChat();
                  }
              }, 3000);

              setTimeout(function() {
                  if (window.agentforce_should_minimize && isChatOpen()) {
                      console.log('💬 [Timed Check] Attempt at 5s');
                      minimizeChat();
                  }
              }, 5000);
          })();

          // Initialize
          if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
              document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initialize);
          } else {
              initialize();
          }

      })();
      // ============================================================
      // END MODAL OVERLAY
      // ============================================================

      (function() {
          'use strict';
          let pendingSearchQuery = null;
          let conversationStarted = false;
          let messageSendAttempts = 0;
          const MAX_SEND_ATTEMPTS = 5;

          document.addEventListener('launchMIAWChat', function(event) {
              const searchQuery = event.detail?.searchQueryParam;
              if (!searchQuery || searchQuery.trim() === '') {
                  return;
              }
              pendingSearchQuery = searchQuery;
              messageSendAttempts = 0;

              try {
                  sessionStorage.setItem('agentforce_search_query', searchQuery);
                  window.agentforce_search_query = searchQuery;
              } catch (e) {
                  console.error('[Agentforce] Error storing search query:', e);
              }
              const portalVariation = getCookie('apex__portalSearchName');
              if (portalVariation !== 'agenticSearch') {
                  return;
              }

              // Check if chat window exists and its state
              const chatFrame = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingFrame');
              const isChatOpen = chatFrame && chatFrame.classList.contains('isMaximized');

              // If conversation is active, send message immediately (works for both open and minimized chat)
              if (conversationStarted && window.embeddedservice_bootstrap?.utilAPI?.sendTextMessage) {
                  console.log('[Agentforce] Conversation already active, sending message immediately');
                  launchChat(searchQuery);
                  // Wait a moment for chat window to open/maximize, then send
                  setTimeout(function() {
                      if (pendingSearchQuery) {
                          console.log('[Agentforce] Sending message via immediate path');
                          sendMessageToAgent(pendingSearchQuery);
                      }
                  }, 800);
              } else if (isChatOpen && !conversationStarted) {
                  // Chat is open but conversation was ended - start new conversation
                  console.log('[Agentforce] Chat window open but conversation ended, starting new conversation');
                  launchChat(searchQuery);
                  // Use retry logic to ensure message gets sent
                  retryMessageSend();
              } else {
                  // Chat is closed or no active conversation - start fresh
                  console.log('[Agentforce] Chat closed, starting new conversation');
                  launchChat(searchQuery);
                  // Use retry logic for new conversation
                  retryMessageSend();
              }
          });

          function sendNotificationToChat(message) {
              if (!window.embeddedservice_bootstrap?.utilAPI) {
                  return false;
              }

              try {
                  window.embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI.sendTextMessage(message);
                  return true;
              } catch (error) {
                  return false;
              }
          }

          // Retry logic to ensure message gets sent after conversation starts
          function retryMessageSend() {
              if (!pendingSearchQuery || messageSendAttempts >= MAX_SEND_ATTEMPTS) {
                  if (messageSendAttempts >= MAX_SEND_ATTEMPTS) {
                      console.error('[Agentforce] Max send attempts reached, giving up');
                      pendingSearchQuery = null;
                  }
                  return;
              }

              messageSendAttempts++;
              console.log('[Agentforce] Retry attempt', messageSendAttempts, 'to send message');

              setTimeout(function() {
                  // If conversationStarted handler already took over, let it handle the send
                  if (conversationStartedHandlerExecuted && greetingTimeoutId) {
                      console.log('[Agentforce] Deferring to conversationStarted handler');
                      return;
                  }

                  // Check if conversation has started
                  if (conversationStarted && pendingSearchQuery) {
                      console.log('[Agentforce] Conversation started, sending message now via retry');
                      sendMessageToAgent(pendingSearchQuery);
                  } else if (pendingSearchQuery) {
                      // Try again
                      console.log('[Agentforce] Conversation not started yet, retrying...');
                      retryMessageSend();
                  }
              }, 1500); // Wait 1.5 seconds between attempts
          }

          let greetingTimeoutId = null;
          let conversationStartedHandlerExecuted = false;

          window.addEventListener('onEmbeddedMessagingConversationStarted', function(event) {
              conversationStarted = true;
              conversationStartedHandlerExecuted = true;

              if (pendingSearchQuery) {
                 

                  // Clear any existing timeout
                  if (greetingTimeoutId) {
                      clearTimeout(greetingTimeoutId);
                      greetingTimeoutId = null;
                  }

                  // Set new timeout - wait for greeting message first
                  greetingTimeoutId = setTimeout(function() {
                      if (pendingSearchQuery) {
                          sendMessageToAgent(pendingSearchQuery);
                      }
                  }, 7000);
              }
          });

          let greetingSent = false;

          window.addEventListener('onEmbeddedMessagingMessage', function(event) {
              if (!greetingSent && pendingSearchQuery && event.detail?.message?.type === 'StaticContent') {
                  if (greetingTimeoutId) {
                      clearTimeout(greetingTimeoutId);
                      greetingTimeoutId = null;
                  }
                  greetingSent = true;
                  setTimeout(function() {
                      if (pendingSearchQuery) {
                          console.log('[Agentforce] Sending message via greeting handler');
                          sendMessageToAgent(pendingSearchQuery);
                      }
                  }, 500);
              }
          });

          // Reset conversation state when conversation ends
          window.addEventListener('onEmbeddedMessagingConversationEnded', function(event) {
              console.log('[Agentforce] Conversation ended, resetting state');
              conversationStarted = false;
              conversationStartedHandlerExecuted = false;
              greetingSent = false;
              pendingSearchQuery = null;
              messageSendAttempts = 0;
              if (greetingTimeoutId) {
                  clearTimeout(greetingTimeoutId);
                  greetingTimeoutId = null;
              }
              console.log('[Agentforce] State reset complete, ready for new conversation');
          });

          // BACKUP: Also reset on our custom event (fires when onEmbeddedMessagingReady is called again)
          window.addEventListener('agentforce_conversation_reset', function(event) {
              console.log('[Agentforce] Detected conversation reset via onEmbeddedMessagingReady event');
              conversationStarted = false;
              conversationStartedHandlerExecuted = false;
              greetingSent = false;
              pendingSearchQuery = null;
              messageSendAttempts = 0;
              if (greetingTimeoutId) {
                  clearTimeout(greetingTimeoutId);
                  greetingTimeoutId = null;
              }
              console.log('[Agentforce] State reset complete via backup method, ready for new conversation');
          });

          function launchChat(searchQuery) {
              if (typeof window.embeddedservice_bootstrap === 'undefined') {
                  waitForEmbeddedService(function() {
                      launchChat(searchQuery);
                  });
                  return;
              }

              const agentforceLocale = getCookie('ContactSupportChatLocale') || 'en_US';

              console.log('[Agentforce Launch] Starting launchChat...');
              console.log('[Agentforce Launch] $A available:', typeof $A !== 'undefined');

              // Check if $A is available
              if (typeof $A === 'undefined') {
                  console.error('[Agentforce Launch] ❌ $A is not defined - cannot get user email');
                  // Continue anyway with just locale
                  embeddedservice_bootstrap.prechatAPI.setHiddenPrechatFields({
                      agentforceLocale: agentforceLocale,
                      UserEmail: '',
                      isAuthenticated: false,
                      siteUserId: ''
                  });

                  if (window.embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI?.launchChat) {
                      window.embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI.launchChat();
                  }
                  return;
              }

              // Get authenticated user email (same as Einstein bot)
              const userEmail = $A.get('$SObjectType.CurrentUser.Email');
              const userId = $A.get('$SObjectType.CurrentUser.Id');

              console.log('[Agentforce Launch] User Email from $A:', userEmail);
              console.log('[Agentforce Launch] User ID from $A:', userId);

              // Build prechat fields
              const prechatFields = {
                  agentforceLocale: agentforceLocale
              };

              // Add email if user is authenticated
              if (userEmail && userEmail !== '' && userEmail !== 'null' && userId && userId !== '') {
                  console.log('[Agentforce Launch] ✅ Authenticated user - adding email to prechat');
                  prechatFields.UserEmail = userEmail;
                  prechatFields.isAuthenticated = true;
                  prechatFields.siteUserId = userId;
              } else {
                  console.log('[Agentforce Launch] Anonymous user - userEmail:', userEmail, 'userId:', userId);
                  prechatFields.UserEmail = '';
                  prechatFields.isAuthenticated = false;
                  prechatFields.siteUserId = '';
              }

              console.log('[Agentforce Launch] Final prechat fields:', prechatFields);
              embeddedservice_bootstrap.prechatAPI.setHiddenPrechatFields(prechatFields);
              console.log('[Agentforce Launch] ✅ setHiddenPrechatFields called');

              if (!window.embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI?.launchChat) {
                  return;
              }

              window.embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI.launchChat();
          }

          function sendMessageToAgent(searchQuery) {
              if (!window.embeddedservice_bootstrap?.utilAPI?.sendTextMessage) {
                  console.error('[Agentforce] sendTextMessage API not available');
                  return false;
              }
              try {
                  const result = window.embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI.sendTextMessage(searchQuery);
                  pendingSearchQuery = null;
                  messageSendAttempts = 0; // Reset attempts on success
                  return true;
              } catch (error) {
                  console.error('[Agentforce] Error sending message:', error);
                  return false;
              }
          }

          function waitForEmbeddedService(callback) {
              let attempts = 0;
              const maxAttempts = 20;
              const checkInterval = setInterval(function() {
                  attempts++;
                  if (typeof window.embeddedservice_bootstrap !== 'undefined') {
                      clearInterval(checkInterval);
                      callback();
                  } else if (attempts >= maxAttempts) {
                      clearInterval(checkInterval);
                  }
              }, 500);
          }

          function getCookie(name) {
              var cookies = document.cookie.split('; ');
              for (var i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {
                  var parts = cookies[i].split('=');
                  if (parts[0] === name) {
                      return decodeURIComponent(parts[1]);
                  }
              }
              return null;
          }

          // Use global getPageName function (already defined globally)

      })();
  </script>

  <!-- Agentic AI knowledge search END - Simplified chat launch -->

<script type="text/javascript">
      // Check if current page should always use standard bot

          const overridePages = ['tech-master-support', 'business']; // Pages that always use standard bot
          const isOverridePage = overridePages.includes(pageName);
          return isOverridePage;
      };
	  
      // Standard chatbot configuration - GLOBAL so it can be reused
      window.__BOT_CONFIG__ = {
                bootstrapMinJs: 'https://mcsg.my.site.com/ESWMcAfeeDigitalAssista1718987617577/assets/js/bootstrap.min.js',
                eswConfigDevName: 'McAfee_Digital_Assistant',

              // Check if bot already exists and is working

              window.__BOT_INITIALIZING__ = true;
		  
		     // Get portal search name - CRITICAL CHECK

                  getCookieValues('csp_user_locale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim() : 'en_US';

              if(portalSearchName === 'agenticSearch' && cspuserLocale === 'en_US' && !shouldUseStandardBotForPage()) {
		  window.__BOT_INITIALIZING__ = false;
                  return; // Exit early, don't initialize standard chatbot
              }

      // CRITICAL: Stop removing elements and unblock bootstrap
      if (window.__ALLOW_STANDARD_BOT__) {
          window.__ALLOW_STANDARD_BOT__();
