      if (window.__UNBLOCK_BOOTSTRAP__) {
          window.__UNBLOCK_BOOTSTRAP__();
		  }
            const chatLocale = getCookieValues('ContactSupportChatLocale') ? getCookieValues('ContactSupportChatLocale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim() : 'en_US';
            const hideChatBot = getCookieValues('hideChatBot')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();
			const akamaiLocale = getCookieValues('ContactSupportChatLocale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();
			const callLocalefromAkamai = getCookieValues('ContactSupportCallLocale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();
            if(window.cookiesCheckCount > 10 || (Boolean(chatLocale) && Boolean(cspuserLocale) && Boolean(hideChatBot))) {  
				    // Use global config
                    const config = window.__BOT_CONFIG__;
					
					// Standard SF Chatbot - Load bootstrap script
					const script = document.createElement('script');
					script.src = config.bootstrapMinJs;
					script.onload = function() {
                          initEmbeddedMessaging();
                          // Reset flag after successful init
                          setTimeout(function() {
                              window.__BOT_INITIALIZING__ = false;
                          }, 2000);
                      };
					  script.onerror = function() {
                          window.__BOT_INITIALIZING__ = false;
                      };
					document.body.appendChild(script);
					if(window.addEventListener) {
						window.addEventListener("message", handleMessage);
					} 
					else {
						window.attachEvent("onmessage", handleMessage);
					}
				
            } else {
                window.cookiesCheckCount += 1;
				window.__BOT_INITIALIZING__ = false; // Reset flag so retry can proceed
                setTimeout(loadBootstrapMinJs, 1000);
            }
        }
		// Start loading
        setTimeout(loadBootstrapMinJs, 1000);
    });
	
	// Global variables
    window.botIncludedPages = ['topic','topiccatalog','article','global-search','case','countries-and-phone'];
    // Utility functions for chatbot operations

    window.v_hideChatBot = "true";
    const checkPreChatFieldsValues = value => value !== undefined && value !== null;
	
	// Utility function needed for the event listener above
      function getPortalSearchNameCookieValue(name) {
          const cookie = document.cookie.split('; ').find(c => c.startsWith(name + '='));
          return cookie ? decodeURIComponent(cookie.split('=')[1]) : '';
      }
	  
    // get Cookie Values
    const getCookieValues = name => {
        const cookie = document.cookie.split('; ').find(c => c.startsWith(name + '='));
        return cookie ? decodeURIComponent(cookie.split('=')[1]) : 'en_US';
    };
	
	//get Bot Cookie Values
	const getBotCookieValue = name => {
		const cookie = document.cookie.split('; ').find(c => c.startsWith(name + '='));
		return cookie ? decodeURIComponent(cookie.split('=')[1]) : '';
	};
	
    // Use global getPageName function
    const getPageName = window.getPageName;
	  
    // Set preChat Hidden fields
    function callPrechatAPI(event) {
          // Skip if this is agenticSearch variation
          const portalSearchName = getPortalSearchNameCookieValue('apex__portalSearchName');
          const cspuserLocale = getCookieValues('csp_user_locale') ?
              getCookieValues('csp_user_locale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim() : 'en_US';
          if(portalSearchName === 'agenticSearch' && cspuserLocale === 'en_US' && !shouldUseStandardBotForPage()) {
              return;
          }
		  
        const akamaiLocale = getCookieValues('ContactSupportChatLocale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();
        const callLocalefromAkamai = getCookieValues('ContactSupportCallLocale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();
	const logs = (event.detail?.userInfo?.email??'No User Info') +'*'+ 
		$A.get('$SObjectType.CurrentUser.Email')+'*'+(event.detail?.queueApiName ?? 'NoQueue');
		
		const userDetails = {
	  siteUserId: $A.get('$SObjectType.CurrentUser.Id'),
	  siteUserEmail: event.detail?.userInfo?.email ?? $A.get('$SObjectType.CurrentUser.Email'),
          AkamaiData: Boolean(getCookieValues('akamaiCountryData')) ? decodeURI(getCookieValues('akamaiCountryData')) : null,
	  botLocale: cspuserLocale,
	  siteLocale: Boolean(akamaiLocale) ? akamaiLocale : 'en_US',
	  callLocale: Boolean(callLocalefromAkamai) ? callLocalefromAkamai : 'en_US',
	  siteUserLanguage: getCookieValues('fallback-language'),
	  queueApiName: event.detail?.queueApiName ?? null,
	  caseId: event.detail?.userInfo?.caseid ?? null,
	  customerAccountId: event.detail?.userInfo?.customeraccountid ?? null,
          setPreviousSessionDetails: event.detail?.userInfo?.caseid ? "true" : "false",
          PageUrl: event.detail?.pageUrl ?? null,
          businessHoursLocale: event.detail?.selectedBizHrsLocale ?? null,
          portalLogs : logs.substring(0, 255)
        };
        Object.entries(userDetails).forEach(([key, value]) => {
            if (checkPreChatFieldsValues(value)) {
                embeddedservice_bootstrap.prechatAPI.setHiddenPrechatFields({ [key]: value });
            }
        });
    };
    // Launch the chat
    const launchChat = async () => {
	          // Skip if this is agenticSearch variation
          const portalSearchName = getPortalSearchNameCookieValue('apex__portalSearchName');
          const cspuserLocale = getCookieValues('csp_user_locale') ?

              // Launch chat
              window.embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI.launchChat();

          }
		  
		const chatLocale = getCookieValues('ContactSupportChatLocale') ? getCookieValues('ContactSupportChatLocale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim() : 'en_US';
		const hideChatBot = getCookieValues('hideChatBot')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();
		const akamaiLocale = getCookieValues('ContactSupportChatLocale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();
		const callLocalefromAkamai = getCookieValues('ContactSupportCallLocale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();
			try {
				await embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI.launchChat();
			} catch (error) {
			} finally {
			}		
		
    };
      
	  // Event listeners for standard chatbot
      window.addEventListener("onEmbeddedMessagingReady", function(event) {

          console.log('[Bot Init] embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI exists:', typeof embeddedservice_bootstrap?.utilAPI !== 'undefined');
          callPrechatAPI(event);

      window.addEventListener("launchChat", launchChat);
      window.addEventListener("onEmbeddedMessagingConversationStarted", (event) => {
      });
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    
    /* START - JAPAN/NON JAPAN ICON LOGIC */
    
    function handleMessage(event) {
        var baseURL = window.location.origin;
        const currentOrigin = 'https://mcsg.my.site.com';

        if(event.origin == currentOrigin && event.data?.botLaunched === 'true') {
            if(getCookieValues('csp_user_locale') == "ja") {
                document.getElementById('embeddedMessagingFrame')?.contentWindow?.postMessage('JapanLocale', '*');
            }
        }

        if (event.data.name === 'hide-chatbot') {
            window.v_hideChatBot = event.data.payload;

            // Polling mechanism to check for embeddedservice_bootstrap
			let attempts = 0;
            const maxAttempts = 40; // 2 seconds max
            var intervalId = setInterval(function() {
				attempts++;
                const chatLocale = getCookieValues('ContactSupportChatLocale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();
                if (typeof embeddedservice_bootstrap !== 'undefined' && typeof embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI !== 'undefined') {
                    clearInterval(intervalId); // Stop polling once embeddedservice_bootstrap is defined
                    if (window.v_hideChatBot == 'false' && (window.botIncludedPages.some(keyword => getPageName() === keyword) || getPageName() == 'home')) {
                        embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI.showChatButton();
                    } else if (window.v_hideChatBot == 'true' || (!window.botIncludedPages.some(keyword => getPageName() === keyword) && getPageName() !== 'home')) {
                        embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI.hideChatButton();
                    }
                } else if (attempts >= maxAttempts) {
                      clearInterval(intervalId);
                 }
            }, 50); // Check every 100 milliseconds
        }
    }

	// Japan vs Non-Japan icon styling
    if(getCookieValues('csp_user_locale') == "ja") {
        var style = document.createElement('style');

  <!-- URL Change Observer - START --> 
<script type="text/javascript">
    let previousUrl = '';
      let botVisibilityIntervalId = null; // Track interval to prevent stacking

      // Use global getPageName function
      const getPageName1 = window.getPageName;
	
		  // Utility function needed for the event listener above
      function getPortalSearchNameCookieValue(name) {
          const cookie = document.cookie.split('; ').find(c => c.startsWith(name + '='));
          return cookie ? decodeURIComponent(cookie.split('=')[1]) : '';
      }

      // Check if current page should always use standard bot
      const shouldUseStandardBotForPage1 = () => {
          const pageName = getPageName1();
          const overridePages = ['tech-master-support', 'business']; // Pages that always use standard bot
          const isOverridePage = overridePages.includes(pageName);
          return isOverridePage;
      };

      const observer = new MutationObserver(function (mutations) {
          if (location.href !== previousUrl) {
              previousUrl = location.href;
              const currentPage = getPageName1();
              // Re-evaluate bot decision for new page (this updates window.__SHOW_AGENTFORCE__ based on current page)
              if (typeof window.evaluateBotDecision === 'function') {
                  window.evaluateBotDecision();
                  console.log('[Nav Observer] Re-evaluated bot decision. __SHOW_AGENTFORCE__:', window.__SHOW_AGENTFORCE__);
              }

              // Check portal search name - EARLY CHECK to protect agenticSearch users
              const portalSearchName = getPortalSearchNameCookieValue('apex__portalSearchName');
              const cspuserLocale = getCookieValues('csp_user_locale') ?
                  getCookieValues('csp_user_locale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim() : 'en_US';

              // Skip standard chatbot logic if agenticSearch
              if(portalSearchName === 'agenticSearch' && cspuserLocale === 'en_US' && !shouldUseStandardBotForPage1()) {
                  console.log('[Nav Observer] ❌ AgenticSearch mode - skipping bot visibility logic');
                  return; // Exit immediately, don't touch anything
              }

			const chatLocale = getCookieValues('ContactSupportChatLocale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();
			const hideChatBot = getCookieValues('hideChatBot')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();	
			
			// Standard chatbot visibility handling
                  // Clear any existing interval before creating new one
                  if (botVisibilityIntervalId) {
                      clearInterval(botVisibilityIntervalId);
                      botVisibilityIntervalId = null;
                  }

                  let attempts = 0;
                  const maxAttempts = 100; // 5 seconds max (100 * 50ms) - increased for bot initialization
				  
            botVisibilityIntervalId = setInterval(function() {
				attempts++;
                const chatLocale = getCookieValues('ContactSupportChatLocale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();
                const hideChatBot = getCookieValues('hideChatBot')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();
				
				// Check if bot is initialized with utilAPI
                if (typeof embeddedservice_bootstrap !== 'undefined' && typeof embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI !== 'undefined') {
                	clearInterval(botVisibilityIntervalId);
                    botVisibilityIntervalId = null;
					
					const shouldHide = hideChatBot == 'true' || (!window.botIncludedPages.some(keyword => getPageName1() === keyword) && getPageName1() !== 'home') || ['tr', 'fi', 'no'].includes(chatLocale);
					
                    if (shouldHide) {
                        embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI.hideChatButton();
                    } 
                    else {
                        embeddedservice_bootstrap.utilAPI.showChatButton();
                    }
            	}
				   // Check if bot button exists in DOM (alternative to utilAPI)
                      else if (document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingConversationButton')) {
                          clearInterval(botVisibilityIntervalId);
                          botVisibilityIntervalId = null;
                          const botButton = document.querySelector('.embeddedMessagingConversationButton');

                          const shouldHide = hideChatBot == 'true' || (!window.botIncludedPages.some(keyword => getPageName1() === keyword) && getPageName1() !== 'home') || ['tr', 'fi', 'no'].includes(chatLocale);

                          if (shouldHide) {
                              // Hide bot by setting display style
                              if (botButton) botButton.style.display = 'none';
                          }
                          else {
                              // Show bot by removing display style
                              if (botButton) botButton.style.display = '';
                          }
                      }
                      else if (attempts >= maxAttempts) {
                          clearInterval(botVisibilityIntervalId);
                          botVisibilityIntervalId = null;

                          // Check if we should show the bot on this page
                          const currentPage = getPageName1();
                          const isPageInBotList = window.botIncludedPages.some(keyword => currentPage === keyword);
                          const isHome = currentPage === 'home';
                          const chatLocale = getCookieValues('ContactSupportChatLocale')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();
                          const hideChatBot = getCookieValues('hideChatBot')?.replace(/-/g, '_')?.trim();
                          const isRestrictedLocale = ['tr', 'fi', 'no'].includes(chatLocale);

                          const shouldShowBot = (hideChatBot !== 'true') && (isPageInBotList || isHome) && !isRestrictedLocale;

                          if (shouldShowBot) {
                              // Trigger bot re-initialization by reloading bootstrap
                              if (typeof window.loadBootstrapMinJs === 'function') {
                                  console.log('[Nav Observer] Calling window.loadBootstrapMinJs()');
                                  setTimeout(function() {
                                      window.loadBootstrapMinJs();
                                  }, 500);
                              } else {
                                  console.error('[Nav Observer] ❌ window.loadBootstrapMinJs not available');
                              }
                          } else {
                              console.log('[Nav Observer] Bot not needed on this page');
                          }
                      }
				}, 50);
        }
    });
    const config = { subtree: true, childList: true };
    observer.observe(document, config);
</script>
  <!-- URL Change Observer - END -->
  <!-- Standard Chatbot Code - END -->

			if (auraConfig.context.dpbp) {
				// Set a data attribute on document.body to signal engine to bypass global patching
				document.body.setAttribute("data-global-patching-bypass", "temporary-bypass");
			}
		}

		// LockerService must be initialized before scripts can be executed.
		$A.lockerService.initialize(auraConfig.context);

		// scripts inside custom templates with Locker active are stored
		// until now since we need LockerService before running

		var scripts = window.Aura.inlineJsLocker;
		if (scripts) {
			for (var i = 0; i < scripts.length; i++) {
				$A.lockerService.runScript(scripts[i]["callback"], scripts[i]["namespace"]);
			}

			delete window.Aura.inlineJsLocker;
		}

		if (true) {
			$A.initAsync(auraConfig);
		} else if (false) {
			$A.initConfig(auraConfig);
		}
	}

}

function closeErrorBox() {
	if (window["$A"]) {
		$A.util.removeClass(auraErrorMask, "auraForcedErrorBox");
		$A.util.removeClass($A.util.getElement("auraErrorReload"), "show");
	} else {
		document.body.removeChild(auraErrorMask);
	}
}
function squash(e) {
	e.preventDefault();
	e.stopPropagation();
}
if (x) {
	x.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
		closeErrorBox();
		squash(e);
	});
}

if (err) {
	err.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
		if (e.key === 'Escape') {
			squash(e);
			closeErrorBox();
		} else if (e.key === 'Tab') {
			// Focus trap
			squash(e);
			if (e.target === x && errorReload && errorReload.classList.contains('show')) {
				errorReload.focus();
			} else if (e.target === errorReload) {
				x.focus();
			}
		}
	});
}

if (auraErrorMask) {
	var errorMaskObserver = new MutationObserver(function(ms) {
		ms.forEach(function(mut) {
			if (mut.type === 'attributes' && mut.attributeName === 'class' && x && auraErrorMask.classList.contains('auraForcedErrorBox')) {
				requestAnimationFrame(function() { x.focus(); });
			}
		});
	});

	errorMaskObserver.observe(auraErrorMask, { attributes: true, attributeFilter: ['class'] });
}

function onLoadStyleSheets(event) {
	if(event){
		var element = event.target;
		element.removeEventListener("load",onLoadStyleSheets);
		element.removeEventListener("error",onLoadStyleSheetsError);
	}
	window.Aura.bootstrap.appCssLoading = (--appCssLoadingCount) > 0;
	if (!window.Aura.bootstrap.appCssLoading) {
		if (typeof window.Aura.bootstrap.appCssLoadedCallback === "function") {
			window.Aura.bootstrap.appCssLoadedCallback();
			window.Aura.bootstrap.appCssLoadedCallback = undefined;
		}
	}
}
function onLoadStyleSheetsError(event) {
	window.Aura.bootstrap.hasCssLoadError = true;
	onLoadStyleSheets(event);
}
